# VitTrade Home UI Rollout Execution Plan

**Status:** Active tracking plan
**Foundation:** `docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/VitTrade-Home-UI-Rollout-Playbook.md`
**Generated:** 2026-06-14
**Scope source:** `flutter_app/lib/features/**/presentation/pages/*.dart`

Autonomous execution prompt:
`docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/AI-Home-UI-Rollout-Autonomous-Execution-Prompt.md`

---

## 1. Objective

Roll out the Home UI standard across the Flutter app without missing screen
entry files and without spending tokens rereading the full repository in every
batch.

This plan tracks **screen entry files** only. Files named `*_part_*.dart` are
implementation details of their parent screen and must not be counted as
separate screens.

Current inventory from source:

```text
screen_entry_files = 390
raw_page_files_including_part_files = 607
test_feature_modules = 22
```

Quality goals:

- Apply the Home hierarchy and shared-component system where the screen pattern
  matches.
- Preserve each module's business logic, routes, providers, copy boundaries,
  financial safety, and domain semantics.
- Do not increase design-token debt or typography debt.
- Work in small batches so the agent only reads the target screens, their local
  widgets, related tests, the playbook, and the shared primitives needed for
  that batch.
- Use GitNexus for dependency and impact discovery before edits so shared
  components, routes, providers, entities, and tests are not missed.

## 1.1 Home Baseline Snapshot

Home is the UI baseline that every rollout batch must protect. If Home source
changes, update this snapshot, the autonomous prompt, the playbook, and related
tests in the same batch.

| Contract | Current baseline |
| --- | --- |
| Audit state | `root_page_bundle_summary` for `home_page.dart` must pass with `totalDebt=0` |
| Page rhythm | compact announcement -> portfolio hero -> next action -> market ticker -> products -> recent -> discovery -> market/full lists |
| Surface order | `HomeSurfaceOrder.productsBeforeRecent` |
| Density policy | `HomeDensityVariant.compact` at width `<= 480`; compact shows `6` primary actions; comfortable shows `9`; overflow actions go into `VitSheetPanel` |
| Announcement policy | Render only active `campaign`, `security`, and `risk` announcements; do not surface `info` announcements on Home; campaign can auto-hide after `96dp`; security/risk must not auto-hide on scroll |
| Shared visual baseline | `VitAnnouncementBanner.compact`, `VitCard.hero`, `VitMetricDeltaPill`, `VitNextActionCard`, `VitMarketTickerStrip`, `VitActionTileGrid.maxVisibleItems`, `VitCompactProductCard`, `VitDiscoveryActionCard.compact`, `VitMarketPairRow`, `VitRankedAssetRow`, `VitAssetAvatar`, `VitSparkline` |
| Guardrail | The Home page bundle must not reintroduce local visual classes, local `Container`, `BoxDecoration`, raw `EdgeInsets`, raw radii, emoji tab labels, or bottom navigation inside Home |

## 1.2 Home Sync Checklist

Use this checklist in every batch that changes Home or any shared primitive
that can affect Home:

- [ ] Home source still preserves the order, density, announcement behavior,
      ticker, and bottom-nav clearance from the snapshot above, or the snapshot
      has been intentionally updated with evidence.
- [ ] `flutter_app/test/features/home/home_page_test.dart` still covers the
      latest contract: products before recent, market ticker tap, announcement
      session behavior, first viewport, and local-pattern guardrails.
- [ ] `docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/AI-Home-UI-Rollout-Autonomous-Execution-Prompt.md`
      and the playbook have been synchronized if the Home baseline changed.
- [ ] Audit evidence still keeps Home at `totalDebt=0`; never modify the audit
      tool to hide debt.

---

## 2. Shared Component Application Standard

Do not force every screen to use **every** shared component in the project. The
correct enterprise standard is to enforce components by **pattern, token, and
safety contract**:

```text
Shared component is mandatory when the screen has the matching UI pattern.
Domain-specific composition stays local when it owns business logic or safety copy.
```

This keeps the UI consistent without breaking specialized UX for auth,
onboarding, advanced charts, fullscreen tools, Arena points-only flows, or
high-risk financial forms.

### Enforcement Levels

| Level | Rule | Required when |
| --- | --- | --- |
| L0 - Token compliance | Use `AppColors`, `AppSpacing`, `AppTextStyles`, and `AppModuleAccents`; do not create local palettes, fonts, spacing, or radii in page bundles | Every screen |
| L1 - Shared layout | Use `VitPageLayout`, `VitPageContent`, `VitHeader`/`VitTopChrome`, `VitInsetScrollView`, `VitCard`, and shared state widgets when available | Any screen with a matching shell, content, card, or state pattern |
| L2 - Pattern shared | Use `VitMarketPairRow`, `VitActionTileGrid`, `VitDiscoveryActionCard`, `VitHighRiskStatePanel`, `VitInput`, `VitTabBar`, and `VitStatusPill` when the pattern matches | Screens with market rows, action launchers, cross-module discovery, high-risk forms, input forms, tabs, or status |
| L3 - Domain local | Keep composition local when it owns business boundaries, provider state, domain copy, route logic, financial safety, or Arena points-only language | When a shared component would blur the domain or pull business logic into `shared/` |

### Hard Rules

- Do not create a local scaffold, header, card, CTA, input, tab, section
  header, status pill, avatar, sparkline, bottom-sheet handle, or state widget
  if a shared primitive already covers the same behavior.
- Do not use local `TextStyle(fontSize: ...)`, raw color, raw spacing, raw
  radius, or raw decoration in page bundles when a token or shared primitive
  covers the need.
- Wallet, Trade, and P2P must preserve masking, fees, risks, limits,
  preview/confirm flows, and next-step copy.
- Market, Trade, Wallet, Earn, DCA, and Launchpad numbers must use
  `AppTextStyles.tabularFigures`.
- Arena is always points-only. Do not use wallet, payout, profit, or
  stake-return language in Arena.
- Prediction Markets keep their own wallet-value language: positions,
  probability, receipt, and P/L. Do not mix this language with Arena.
- Module pages must not copy `VitTopChromeType.rootBrand` from Home unless the
  page is a true app-root surface.

### Soft Rules

- If a pattern appears on only one screen and clearly owns business logic, keep
  it local first.
- If the same visual pattern appears on 2-3 screens or in 2 modules, create or
  extend a domain-neutral shared component.
- New guardrails should start as advisory if many legacy variants still exist;
  make them strict only after migration proves the shared component works.
- Do not refactor route, provider, or business logic only to apply a shared
  component.

### Allowed Exceptions

| Exception | Reason |
| --- | --- |
| Auth/onboarding | May need fullscreen or no-bottom-nav flows that differ from Home |
| Advanced chart/fullscreen workspace | Canvas/tool interaction can be more important than card/page rhythm |
| Dev/admin preview tools | May need to show many primitives at once for design-system QA |
| Financial confirmation with domain-specific copy | Safety copy and route logic must stay in the feature layer |
| Arena/Prediction bridge surfaces | Boundary language must stay explicit and must not become one shared business card |

A batch is aligned only when the implementer can name the level used for every
screen: L0/L1 are always checked, L2 is applied when the pattern matches, and
L3 is recorded with a reason when local composition remains.

---

## 3. Token-Efficient Workflow

Use this workflow for every implementation batch:

1. Choose one module and 2-5 screen entry files from the inventory below.
2. Read only those screens, their local widgets, related tests, and the shared
   primitives they already use.
3. Map each screen to one playbook pattern:
   `command center`, `financial hero`, `market/data list`, `high-risk form`,
   `confirmation/receipt`, `profile/settings`, `points-only/social`, or
   `support/info`.
4. Apply mandatory L0/L1, apply L2 when the pattern matches, and record the
   reason when L3 local composition remains.
5. Preserve routes, providers, keys, masking, fee/risk/limit copy, and
   Prediction/Arena boundaries.
6. Run GitNexus `impact` before modifying any shared widget, route, provider,
   controller, entity, repository contract, or helper used outside the target
   screen.
7. After edits, run GitNexus `detect_changes` to record actual blast radius.
8. Use MCP Headroom only when long GitNexus output, analyzer logs, test logs,
   audit output, route reports, or diffs would crowd out the active context.
   Record Headroom hashes if used.
9. Run focused tests for the module and token-audit checks.
10. Update the batch log with `Home pattern applied`, `L3 local reason`,
   `GitNexus evidence`, `first viewport evidence`, and `tests/audit evidence`
   before moving to the next batch.

### Mandatory GitNexus Workflow

Before the first batch:

```bash
node .gitnexus/run.cjs status
node .gitnexus/run.cjs analyze
```

Run `analyze` only when the index is stale, missing, corrupt, or GitNexus
returns unreliable answers. In each batch:

1. Use `list_repos` to confirm the indexed repository.
2. Use `context` for each screen class in the batch.
3. Use `query` when you need to find module ownership, execution flows, or
   related shared primitives.
4. Use `impact` before edits to shared, router, provider, controller, or entity
   code.
5. Use `detect_changes` after edits to record affected symbols and processes.

GitNexus does not replace source, tests, or audits. If the graph is stale or
missing edges, inspect source directly and record the limitation in batch notes.

### MCP Headroom Policy

Headroom is optional and should be used only to manage long context. It does
not replace source files, tests, audits, GitNexus, or this execution plan.

Use Headroom for:

- Long GitNexus `context`, `impact`, or `detect_changes` output.
- Long analyzer, test, audit, route, or diff output that may need later lookup.
- Previous-batch evidence that is useful for continuity after it has been
  recorded permanently in this plan.

Do not use Headroom for:

- The autonomous prompt, this execution plan, or the playbook.
- Current source files that must be edited or verified from disk.
- Financial safety rules, Prediction/Arena boundary rules, or Definition of
  Done.

When Headroom is used, record the relevant hashes in batch notes:

```text
Headroom refs: impact=<hash>, test-log=<hash>, audit=<hash>
```

Do not ask an AI agent to "fix the whole app UI" in one prompt. Use a small
batch prompt like this:

```text
Target docs:
- docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/VitTrade-Home-UI-Rollout-Playbook.md
- docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/VitTrade-Home-UI-Rollout-Execution-Plan.md

Target module:
- <module>

Target screens:
- <screen_1.dart>
- <screen_2.dart>

Required behavior:
- Use Home-derived shared components.
- Keep business logic/safety unchanged.
- Use GitNexus context/impact/detect_changes and record evidence.
- Use Headroom for long outputs only; record hashes if used.
- Update tests/audit evidence.
```

---

## 4. Priority And Batch Rules

| Priority | Modules | Reason | Batch size | Required verification |
| --- | --- | --- | ---: | --- |
| P0 | `wallet`, `trade`, `p2p` | Money movement, orders, escrow, account safety | 2-4 screens | Focused module tests, design-token audit, high-risk guardrail when applicable |
| P1 | `markets`, `profile`, `auth`, `onboarding`, `notifications`, `support` | Primary navigation, account/security, first-run trust | 3-5 screens | Focused module tests, top-header guardrails if header changes |
| P2 | `predictions`, `arena`, `earn`, `dca`, `launchpad` | Product depth, boundary-sensitive copy, dense cards/lists | 3-5 screens | Focused module tests, copy-boundary review, responsive QA for grids/forms |
| P3 | `discovery`, `cross_module`, `referral`, `rewards`, `news`, `admin`, `dev`, `enterprise_states` | Secondary/internal surfaces after main product flows | 4-6 screens | Focused tests or nearest tests, full suite if shared previews change |
| Done | `home` | Source foundation already aligned | N/A | Keep Home root bundle `totalDebt=0` |

Status values:

| Status | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| `Not started` | Home-standard rollout has not started for this screen/module. |
| `In progress` | Rollout has started or some root bundles are clean, but root-bundle debt or audit coverage gaps remain. |
| `Blocked` | Product/design decision or shared primitive gap is blocking progress. |
| `Done` | The screen was migrated, evidence was recorded, and no safety regression exists. |
| `Deferred` | Intentionally postponed, usually because the surface is internal, obsolete, or demo-only. |

## 5.2 Next Batch Queue

Use this queue when resuming the rollout from the 2026-06-18 actual audit
snapshot. Do not jump to a later item until the earlier item is `Done`,
`Blocked`, or `Deferred` with evidence in the batch log. After every batch,
rerun `dart run tool/design_token_consistency_audit.dart --check`, update
section `5.1` if counts changed, and refresh this queue if the next target
changes.

Coverage gaps are part of the rollout. A module is not `Done` if an inventory
screen is outside `root_page_bundle_summary`, even when covered root bundles
have `totalDebt=0`.

No remaining queue items in the current audit snapshot. If a later audit
introduces new root-bundle debt or coverage gaps, add the next batch here with
evidence before editing.

Copy this row into the log when a new implementation batch starts. Do not mark
`Done` if any of these are missing: Home pattern, L3 reason, GitNexus evidence,
first-viewport evidence, or tests/audit evidence. If Headroom was used, record
its hashes in the notes.

---

## 8. Required Commands By Change Type

Docs-only tracking update:

```bash
git diff --check -- docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/VitTrade-Home-UI-Rollout-Execution-Plan.md
```

GitNexus preflight from repository root:

```bash
node .gitnexus/run.cjs status
node .gitnexus/run.cjs analyze
```

Single-module UI batch:

```bash
cd flutter_app
dart run tool/design_token_consistency_audit.dart --check
flutter test test/quality/design_token_consistency_guardrail_test.dart --reporter=compact
flutter analyze
flutter test test/features/<module> --reporter=compact
```

Shared primitive or cross-module batch:

```bash
cd flutter_app
dart run tool/design_token_consistency_audit.dart --check
flutter analyze
flutter test --reporter=compact
```

Run emulator or responsive visual QA when a batch changes first viewport,
bottom chrome clearance, dense grids, high-risk forms, or market rows.
